DFDuck's #AmiWestTA IRC Conference Logs 11-Jul-98

This is my complete log. Unaltered other than editing out my private messages, reformatting of text to make it readable (ever try reading an AmIRC log?), and adding html tags top and bottom. I missed the beginning of both days. I started logging at 1:15pm the 11th and 10:26am the 12th. If anyone has those times logged I would really appreciate a copy of them.
